A @FEMA Mobile Emergency Response Support (MERS) unit is deploying with secure &amp; non-secure voice,video &amp; information services to support emergency response communications needs. Additional FEMA mobile communications vehicles are also being deployed as requested. #Sayfie
The Department of Energy activated its Energy Response Organization. DOE is coordinating with industry to activate mutual assistance network. Crews from 19 states have mobilized to restore power as soon as it is safe. DOE is also monitoring the availability of fuel. #Sayfie
U.S. Army Corps of Engineer's is Deploying a Temporary Power Planning &amp; Response Team (PRT) &amp; members from the 249th Engineer Battalion to provide temporary emergency power in Florida.  Additional PRTs have been placed on alert. #Sayfie
U.S. Health &amp; Human Services has 3 teams of medical personnel from the National Disaster Medical System (NDMS) along with an Incident Management Team ready to go. More than 125 personnel have been deployed. 5 Ambulance strike teams are mobilizing as well. #sayfie
.@USCG has pre-staged fixed &amp; rotary wing aircraft for response. Also 8 shallow water rescue teams are ready with 10 additional teams on standby; 5 boats pre-positioned for support with five more on standby; &amp;16 cutters positioned to assist with Search &amp; Rescue #Sayfie
.@DeptofDefense has prepared ground transportation/high-water capable vehicles to move personnel &amp; cargo in the affected areas. Will also provide rotary wing aircraft, swift water boats &amp; rescue personnel. Working to make them available to deploy as this evening #Sayfie
